- Confirmation email with fundraiser link
- Dashboard access to track
- Share templates sent via email

***

## 🚨 **WHAT TO AVOID (Donor POV):**

❌ **Don't overwhelm with options** - ONE cause (animal shelter) for now
❌ **Don't make long forms** - 5-7 fields max
❌ **Don't hide the "what if I don't reach goal" answer** - address this fear upfront
❌ **Don't forget social proof** - show other fundraisers if possible
❌ **Don't skip share templates** - most people don't know what to say
❌ **Don't be vague about "what you get"** - spell out the link, dashboard, updates

***

## 📊 **KEY DIFFERENCES: CSR vs FUNDRAISER PAGE:**

| **Element** | **CSR Page** | **Fundraiser Page** |
| :-- | :-- | :-- |
| **Audience** | Corporate decision-makers | Individual millennials/Gen Z |
| **Tone** | Professional, formal | Warm, personal, emotional |
| **Goal** | Schedule consultation call | Create fundraiser immediately |
| **Trust Signals** | Legal compliance, audits | Friend testimonials, tax benefit |
| **Length** | Lean, scannable | Can be slightly longer (more hand-holding needed) |
| **Visuals** | Corporate/professional | Emotional, personal, animals |
| **CTA** | "Request Consultation" | "Start My Fundraiser" |

# is this correct english for the csr page - yes or no answer

Implementation, reporting, measurable results

**NO**

Should be: "Implementation, reporting, **and** measurable results"

(Need "and" before the last item in a list of three or more - it's called the Oxford comma/serial comma rule)

---

# so how come you wrote wrong

You're absolutely right to call me out! I made an inconsistency error.

**In the CSR page, I wrote:**
"Implementation, reporting, measurable results" ❌ (missing "and")

**But I should have written:**
"Implementation, reporting, and measurable results" ✅

**Why I did this:**
I was trying to keep it ultra-short and punchy (marketing style), but grammatically it's incorrect without the "and."

**Should I fix it in the CSR page?**

It should read:
**"3. Impact** – Implementation, reporting, **and** measurable results"

Want me to update the CSR page final content with this correction?

## **DESIGN SPECIFICATIONS FOR DESIGNER:**

### **Typography:**

- **Headings:** Helvetica Bold, 16-18pt
- **Subheadings:** Helvetica Bold, 12-14pt
- **Body Text:** Helvetica Regular, 10-11pt
- **Footer/Small Text:** Helvetica Regular, 8-9pt


### **Colors:**

- **Primary Text:** Black (\#000000)
- **Secondary Text:** Dark Grey (\#333333 or \#555555)
- **Accents:** Brand accent color (for highlights, icons)
- **Background:** White with optional light grey (\#F5F5F5) for section boxes


### **Layout:**

- Clean, generous white space
- Avoid clutter - this is corporate-facing
- Use subtle borders or light grey boxes to separate sections if needed
- Align text consistently (left-aligned preferred for body text)


### **Icons:**

- Use simple, professional icons (checkmarks, numbers, contact icons)
- Consistent style throughout (line icons or solid icons, not mixed)
- Brand color or black/grey


### **Logo:**

- RKM Foundation logo on top left of both pages
- Not too large, but clearly visible


### **Professional Touch:**

- This PDF will be forwarded to CFOs/CEOs - keep it polished
- Print-friendly (black and white should also look good)
- No heavy graphics that distract from content

## 🎯 **FUNDRAISER PAGE - DONOR POV REVIEW**

Let me put on my "18-year-old planning birthday fundraiser" hat...

***

## 🚨 **WHAT'S WRONG (Honest Assessment):**

### **1. TOO FORMAL/ADULT LANGUAGE**

**Current:** "Turn your special day into impact"
**Problem:** Sounds like LinkedIn. 15-25 year olds don't talk like this.

**Current:** "Create a legacy of compassion"
**Problem:** Too heavy. I'm 20, not writing my will.

***

### **2. "INSTEAD OF GIFTS" = AWKWARD**

**Current:** "Celebrate your birthday by vaccinating shelter dogs or feeding animals for a day **instead of receiving gifts**"

**Problem:**

- Makes me sound preachy to friends
- What if I still want gifts? Now I feel guilty.
- Forces me to explain "I don't want your gifts"

**Better approach:** Focus on ADDING something meaningful, not REPLACING gifts.

***

### **3. MISSING THE "HOW MUCH SHOULD I ASK FOR?"**

**Current:** Shows ₹7L total shelter goal
**Problem:** I have no idea what MY personal goal should be.

**What I need:** "Most fundraisers set goals between ₹5,000-₹25,000" or "Aditya raised ₹25,000 for his birthday"

***

### **4. NO CHOICE IN WHAT MY FUNDRAISER SUPPORTS**

**Current:** Generic "animal shelter"
**Problem:** I can't tell my friends "Your ₹1,000 will feed 2 dogs" - it's vague.

**What I need:** Let me choose:

- [ ] Daily feeding program
- [ ] Vaccinations
- [ ] Medical care
- [ ] Kennel construction
- [ ] General shelter support

This gives me a STORY to tell friends.

***

### **5. "IMPORTANT TO KNOW" SOUNDS SCARY**

**Current:** Legal compliance paragraph
**Problem:** Makes me think "Wait, can I get in trouble?"

**Better:** Rename to "How it works safely" or soften the tone.

***

### **6. MISSING: "WHAT DO I SAY TO MY FRIENDS?"**

**Current:** Just says "share your link"
**Problem:** I'm 18. I don't know what to write. I feel awkward asking for money.

**What I need:** Copy-paste templates for WhatsApp, Instagram caption, birthday post.

***

### **7. FAQ MISSES KEY TEEN CONCERNS**

**Missing questions:**

- "Will this look weird to my friends?"
- "What if only 2 people donate?"
- "Do I have to tell everyone how much I raised?"
- "Can I donate to my own fundraiser?"

***

## ✅ **REWRITTEN FUNDRAISER PAGE (Donor-Friendly, 15+ Audience)**


***

### **SECTION 1: HERO**

**Headline:**
Celebrate with purpose

**Subheadline:**
Turn your birthday, anniversary, or milestone into a fundraiser for rescued animals. Easy to set up, meaningful to share.

**Primary CTA:**
Start Your Fundraiser

**Visual:** Happy, relatable person (teen/20s) with rescued animals OR celebration + animals vibe

**Design Note:** Warm, friendly, not corporate. Use friendly font weight.

***

### **SECTION 2: HOW IT WORKS**

**Headline:**
How it works

**3 Steps:**

**1. Create**
Set your goal and choose what you're raising funds for (feeding, vaccinations, medical care, etc.)

**2. Share**
We give you a link and message templates. Share on WhatsApp, Instagram, or anywhere you like.

**3. Track \& celebrate**
Watch donations come in. We'll send you updates on the impact you created.

***

### **SECTION 3: WHY FUNDRAISE WITH RKM**

**Headline:**
Why people choose RKM Foundation

✓ **You're in control**
Set your own goal. Choose what your fundraiser supports. It's your celebration, your way.

✓ **Easy for your friends**
They donate in 2 clicks. Instant payment. Automatic tax receipt (80G benefit).

✓ **See the impact**
Real updates with photos and stories of the animals you helped.

✓ **Safe \& transparent**
All funds go directly to RKM Foundation's animal shelter. No third parties. Fully secure.

***

### **SECTION 4: CHOOSE WHAT YOU SUPPORT**

**Headline:**
What will your fundraiser support?

When you create your fundraiser, pick what speaks to you:

**🍖 Daily Feeding Program**
₹2,000 feeds one dog for a month

**💉 Vaccinations \& Deworming**
₹800 vaccinates one animal

**🩺 Medical Care \& Treatment**
₹3,000-₹10,000 for emergency treatment or surgery

**🏠 Kennel Construction**
₹8,000 builds one kennel for a rescued animal

**🐾 General Shelter Support**
Your funds go where they're needed most

**Design Note:** Use emojis or icons. Make it visual and scannable. Let them choose during fundraiser setup.

***

### **SECTION 5: FUNDRAISER IDEAS**

**Headline:**
Fundraiser ideas

**4 Cards:**

**🎂 Birthday fundraiser**
"This year, I'm celebrating by helping rescued animals. Join me?"

**💍 Anniversary or milestone**
"For our anniversary, we're supporting the animal shelter instead of gifts."

**🏃 Fitness challenge**
"Every kilometer I run, animals get fed. Sponsor my challenge!"

**💙 Just because**
"No special occasion needed. Let's help some furry friends together."

**Design Note:** Remove "instead of receiving gifts" language. Focus on ADDING purpose, not replacing.

***

### **SECTION 6: WHAT YOU GET**

**Headline:**
What you get

✓ **Your own fundraiser page**
With your name, photo, and personal message

✓ **Easy share tools**
Copy-paste messages for WhatsApp, Instagram, Facebook

✓ **Live updates**
See who donated and how close you are to your goal

✓ **Impact proof**
Photos and stories of the animals your fundraiser helped

✓ **Tax receipts for donors**
Everyone gets instant 80G receipt (50% tax benefit)

***

### **SECTION 7: NOT SURE WHAT TO SAY?**

**Headline:**
Not sure what to say? We've got you.

**Body Copy:**
Asking friends to donate can feel awkward. We get it. That's why we give you message templates you can copy-paste or customize.

**Example WhatsApp Message (in grey box):**

> Hey! This year for my birthday, I'm raising funds for RKM Foundation's animal shelter. 🐾
>
> Your donation helps feed, vaccinate, and care for rescued dogs and cats.
>
> Even ₹500 makes a real difference. Plus you get a tax receipt!
>
> [Your fundraiser link here]
>
> Thanks for being part of this! ❤️

**Example Instagram Caption (in grey box):**

> This birthday, I'm doing something different 🐶
>
> Raising funds for rescued animals with @rkmfoundation. Every rupee helps feed, treat, and shelter animals who need it most.
>
> Link in bio or DM me! Even small donations add up. Let's do this together 🙌

**Design Note:** Make templates copy-pasteable. Show them in phone-style message bubbles for realism.

***

### **SECTION 8: HOW IT WORKS SAFELY**

**Headline:**
How it works safely

**Body Copy:**
To keep fundraisers safe and compliant with Indian laws, all funds go directly to RKM Foundation's animal shelter programs that we run and monitor.

You can't create fundraisers for other causes or upload unrelated content. This protects you, your donors, and the animals.

Simple, safe, transparent.

***

### **SECTION 9: CTA**

**Headline:**
Ready to start?

**Body Copy:**
Create your fundraiser in 2 minutes. Pick your goal, personalize your message, and start sharing.

**CTA Button:**
Start Your Fundraiser

***

### **SECTION 10: FAQ**

**Headline:**
Questions? We've got answers.

**Q: What should my fundraiser goal be?**
A: Most people set goals between ₹5,000-₹25,000 for personal fundraisers. Pick what feels right for your friend circle. Remember, every rupee helps!

**Q: What if I don't reach my goal?**
A: Totally fine! Whatever you raise still helps animals. There's no "all or nothing."

**Q: Will this look weird to my friends?**
A: Nope! Fundraisers for birthdays and milestones are super common now. You're doing something cool, not weird.

**Q: What if only a few people donate?**
A: That's still impact! Even ₹2,000 feeds a dog for a month. Small numbers matter.

**Q: Can I donate to my own fundraiser?**
A: Yes! Many people kickstart their fundraiser with their own donation.

**Q: Do I have to share how much I raised?**
A: Nope, that's totally up to you. Your dashboard shows totals, but you decide what to share publicly.

**Q: How do my friends donate?**
A: They click your link, pick an amount, pay via UPI/card (takes 30 seconds), and get instant receipt.

**Q: Can I close my fundraiser early?**
A: Yes, you can close it anytime from your dashboard.

***

### **SECTION 11: NEED HELP**

**Text:**
Need help? Questions? Stuck?
WhatsApp us: +91 99207 80005
Or email: info@rkm.support

**Design Note:** Make WhatsApp number prominent. Teens prefer WhatsApp over email.

***

## 📊 **KEY CHANGES SUMMARY:**

| **What Changed** | **Why** |
| :-- | :-- |
| "Turn special day into impact" → "Celebrate with purpose" | Less formal, more relatable |
| Removed "instead of receiving gifts" | Less awkward, not guilt-trippy |
| Added "Choose what you support" section | Gives specific causes (feeding, vaccines, kennels) |
| Added "Not sure what to say?" with templates | Solves \#1 teen concern (what do I write?) |
| Changed "Important to Know" → "How it works safely" | Less scary, more reassuring |
| Added teen-specific FAQs | "Will this look weird?" "What if only 2 people donate?" |
| WhatsApp number prominent | Teens prefer WhatsApp over email |
| Emojis in fundraiser ideas | Makes it feel friendly, not corporate |
| "Track \& celebrate" instead of just "Impact" | More positive, less preachy |


***

## ✅ **DOES THIS WORK BETTER?**

**Target audience:** 15-30 year olds
**Tone:** Friendly, supportive, not preachy
**Length:** ~450 words (slightly longer but easier to read)
**Key fix:** Removed awkward "instead of gifts" language, added choice of specific causes, included message templates

**Approve or adjust?**

---

## 🎯 **STUDYING YOUR POINTS + DONOR LENS CHECK**

Let me analyze your corrections and rework with 15-30 year old donor perspective...

***

## 🧠 **KEY INSIGHTS FROM YOUR NOTES:**

### **1. NEUTERING COSTS ARE SIGNIFICANT**

- Male neutering: ₹1,800 + ₹1,000 post-op = ₹2,800
- Female neutering: ₹4,800 + ₹2,100 post-op = ₹6,900
- This MUST be a fundraiser option (controls population, prevents suffering)


### **2. COSTS ARE SIMILAR FOR DOGS \& CATS**

- Feeding: ₹2,000/month (both)
- Vaccination: ~₹800-₹1,800 (range)
- Medical emergencies: ₹5,000-₹10,000
- **Solution:** Combine as "dogs and cats" not separate


### **3. "INSTEAD OF GIFTS" STILL APPEARS**

- Anniversary example still has this language
- Need to reframe as "celebrating by supporting" not "replacing gifts"


### **4. "AWKWARD" → "INSPIRATIONAL"**

- Section 7 needs positive reframe
- Donor doesn't want to feel it's awkward to ask
- Make it feel PROUD to ask


### **5. FOOTER CONTACT → CHECK FAQS FIRST**

- Hierarchy: FAQs → Email → WhatsApp
- Reduces support burden, empowers self-service

***

## ✅ **DONOR LENS FINAL CHECK:**

**15-year-old perspective:**

- ✅ Language feels friendly, not corporate
- ✅ "Will this look weird?" FAQ addresses my fear
- ✅ Message templates solve "what do I say?"

- ✅ No pressure to hit goal ("totally fine" language)

**25-year-old perspective:**

- ✅ Anniversary option doesn't force "no gifts" narrative
- ✅ Fitness challenge option feels active/engaging
- ✅ Tax receipt mentioned (I care about this now)
- ✅ "Just because" option for any time (not just milestones)

**Parent perspective (if teen wants to do this):**

- ✅ "How it works safely" section reassures me
- ✅ No third-party causes = less risk
- ✅ Clear what money goes to (feeding, neutering, medical)
- ✅ Can close fundraiser anytime (gives control)

# 📋 **FUNDRAISER PAGE - 3 FINAL IMPLEMENTATION SHEETS**


***

# **SHEET 1: DESIGNER IMPLEMENTATION**


***

## **FUNDRAISER PAGE - COMPLETE DESIGN BRIEF**

### **PAGE OVERVIEW:**

- **Goal:** Get 15-30 year olds to create personal fundraisers for animal shelter
- **Style:** Warm, friendly, youth-oriented (NOT corporate)
- **Length:** Single scroll page (~500 words)
- **Mobile-first:** 70%+ traffic expected on mobile (teens/young adults)

***

### **BRAND GUIDELINES:**

- **Fonts:** Helvetica (all weights) - same as site standard
- **Colors:** Black, White, Grey (primary) + warm accent for CTAs
- **Tone:** Friendly, supportive, positive (no guilt, no pressure)
- **Emojis:** YES - use throughout (friendly, relatable)
- **Layout:** Generous white space, easy to scan

***

## **SECTION-BY-SECTION CONTENT \& DESIGN SPECS:**


***

### **SECTION 1: HERO**

**Headline:**
Celebrate with purpose

**Subheadline:**
Turn your birthday, anniversary, or milestone into a fundraiser for rescued animals. Easy to set up, meaningful to share.

**Primary CTA:**
Start Your Fundraiser

**Visual Element:**
Happy, relatable person (teen/20s) with rescued animals OR celebration + animals vibe (birthday/milestone feel)

**Design Notes:**

- Warm, friendly vibe (NOT corporate like CSR page)
- Use lighter font weight for friendliness
- Hero image should feel personal, not stock-corporate
- CTA button warm color (not corporate blue/grey)
- Mobile: Stacked layout, CTA prominent

***

### **SECTION 2: HOW IT WORKS**

**Section Headline:**
How it works

**3-Step Process:**

**1. Create**
Set your goal and choose what you're raising funds for (feeding, neutering, medical care, shelter, etc.)

**2. Share**
We give you a link and message templates. Share on WhatsApp, Instagram, or anywhere you like.

**3. Track \& celebrate**
Watch donations come in. We'll send you updates on the impact you created.

**Design Notes:**

- Numbered icons (1, 2, 3) with friendly style
- Horizontal on desktop, vertical on mobile
- Icons: 1-Create/edit, 2-Share/social, 3-Chart/celebrate
- Keep compact and scannable
- Use friendly colors (not corporate grey)

***

### **SECTION 3: WHY FUNDRAISE WITH RKM**

**Section Headline:**
Why people choose RKM Foundation

**4 Benefit Points (Checkmark + Text):**

✓ **You're in control**
Set your own goal. Choose what your fundraiser supports. It's your celebration, your way.

✓ **Easy for your friends and family**
They donate in 2 clicks. Instant payment. Automatic tax receipt (80G benefit).

✓ **See the impact**
Real updates with photos and stories of the animals you helped.

✓ **Safe \& transparent**
All funds go directly to RKM Foundation's animal shelter. No third parties. Fully secure.

**Design Notes:**

- Checkmarks in warm/friendly color
- 2x2 grid on desktop, stacked on mobile
- Bold the benefit title (You're in control, Easy for friends, etc.)
- Generous spacing, not cramped
- Icon + text left-aligned

***

> Hey! This year for my birthday, I'm raising funds for RKM Foundation's animal shelter. 🐾

### **SECTION 8: HOW IT WORKS SAFELY**

**Section Headline:**
How it works safely

**Body Copy:**
To keep fundraisers safe and compliant with Indian laws, all funds go directly to RKM Foundation's animal shelter programs that we run and monitor.

You can't create fundraisers for other causes or upload unrelated content. This protects you, your donors, and the animals.

Simple, safe, transparent.

**Design Notes:**

- Simple text block
- Optional: Light grey background box
- Not scary, just informative
- Keep it short and reassuring

***

### **SECTION 9: CTA**

**Section Headline:**
Ready to start?

**Body Copy:**
Create your fundraiser in 2 minutes. Pick your goal, personalize your message, and start sharing.

**CTA Button:**
Start Your Fundraiser

**Design Notes:**

- Large, prominent CTA button
- Warm, inviting color
- Full-width on mobile
- Centered on desktop

***

### **SECTION 10: FAQ**

**Section Headline:**
Questions? We've got answers.

**8 Q\&As (Accordion/Expandable Format Recommended):**

**Q: What should my fundraiser goal be?**
A: Most people set goals between ₹5,000-₹25,000 for personal fundraisers. Pick what feels right for your friend circle. Remember, every rupee helps!

**Q: What if I don't reach my goal?**
A: Totally fine! Whatever you raise still helps animals. There's no "all or nothing."

**Q: Will this look weird to my friends?**
A: Nope! Fundraisers for birthdays and milestones are super common now. You're doing something cool, not weird.

**Q: What if only a few people donate?**
A: That's still impact! Even ₹2,000 feeds a dog or cat for a month. Small numbers matter.

**Q: Can I donate to my own fundraiser?**
A: Yes! Many people kickstart their fundraiser with their own donation.

**Q: Do I have to share how much I raised?**
A: Nope, that's totally up to you. Your dashboard shows totals, but you decide what to share publicly.

**Q: How do my friends donate?**
A: They click your link, pick an amount, pay via UPI/card (takes 30 seconds), and get instant receipt.

**Q: Can I close my fundraiser early?**
A: Yes, you can close it anytime from your dashboard.

**Design Notes:**

- Accordion format (click question to expand answer)
- All collapsed by default
- +/- icons to show expand/collapse state
- Mobile-friendly tap targets
- Keep it scannable

***

### **SECTION 11: NEED HELP**

**Section Headline:**
Have questions?

**Body Copy:**
Check our FAQs above, or reach out to us directly.

📧 **Email:** info@rkm.support
💬 **WhatsApp:** [Chat with Us Button]

**WhatsApp Link:** https://wa.me/919920780005

**Design Notes:**

- WhatsApp button prominent (green \#25D366, WhatsApp icon)
- Email clickable (mailto: link)
- WhatsApp preferred placement (teens use WhatsApp more)
- Clean, simple layout

***

## **RESPONSIVE DESIGN REQUIREMENTS:**

### **Desktop (1200px+):**

- Hero image + text side-by-side OR full-width hero with text overlay
- "Why Fundraise" 2x2 grid
- "Choose What You Support" 2-3 columns
- "Fundraiser Ideas" 2x2 grid


### **Mobile (< 768px):**

- All sections single-column, stacked
- CTA buttons full-width
- Accordions/dropdowns for templates and FAQs (save space)
- Touch targets minimum 44px height
- WhatsApp button sticky or prominent (easy access)

***

## **VISUAL ASSETS NEEDED:**

1. **Hero Image:** Relatable teen/20-something with rescued animals OR birthday/celebration + animals vibe
2. **Emojis/Icons:** 🎂💍🏃💙🍖💉✂️🩺🏠🐾 (or icon equivalents)

4. **Checkmark Icons:** For benefits sections
5. **WhatsApp Icon:** For contact button

- NO guilt ("instead of gifts")
- NO pressure ("totally fine if you don't reach goal")

- Youth-oriented, not corporate

## **FUNDRAISER PAGE - TECHNICAL IMPLEMENTATION**

### **PAGE FUNCTIONALITY:**

#### **1. "Start Your Fundraiser" CTA Behavior:**

**On Click:**

- Opens fundraiser creation form (new page OR modal/overlay)
- URL: `/fundraiser/create` OR modal on same page

**What happens:**

- User fills form (see Form Fields below)
- Submits → Gets unique fundraiser link instantly
- Receives email with link + share templates

***

### **2. FUNDRAISER CREATION FORM:**

#### **Form Fields:**

| Field Name | Type | Validation | Required | Max Length | Notes |
| :-- | :-- | :-- | :-- | :-- | :-- |
| Your Name | Text | Letters, spaces only | Yes | 100 chars | Publicly visible on fundraiser page |
| Email | Email | Valid email format | Yes | 100 chars | For link delivery + updates |
| Phone | Phone | +91 format, 10 digits | Yes | 13 chars | For contact/updates |
| Occasion | Dropdown | Pre-set options | Yes | - | Birthday / Anniversary / Fitness Challenge / Just Because / Other |
| Fundraiser Goal | Dropdown + Custom | Pre-set + custom input | Yes | - | ₹5,000 / ₹10,000 / ₹25,000 / ₹50,000 / Custom Amount |
| Custom Goal Amount | Number | If "Custom" selected | Conditional | 8 digits | Min ₹1,000, Max ₹10,00,000 |
| What are you raising funds for? | Dropdown | Pre-set options | Yes | - | Monthly Feeding / Vaccinations / Neutering / Medical Emergencies / Shelter Support / Where Needed Most |
| Personal Message | Textarea | Any text | No | 500 chars | "Tell your friends why this matters to you" |

**Dropdown Options Detail:**

**Occasion:**

- Birthday
- Anniversary
- Fitness Challenge
- Just Because
- Other

**Fundraiser Goal:**

- ₹5,000
- ₹10,000
- ₹25,000
- ₹50,000
- Custom Amount (opens number input field)

**What are you raising funds for?:**

- 🍖 Monthly Feeding (₹2,000 per animal)
- 💉 Vaccinations (₹2,000 for two animals)
- ✂️ Neutering \& Post-Op Care (₹3,000 male / ₹7,000 female)
- 🩺 Medical Emergency Fund (₹5,000 per animal)
- 🏠 Shelter Support (₹10,000 per kennel)
- 🐾 Where Needed Most

***

### **FORM VALIDATION:**

**Client-Side:**

- All required fields must be filled
- Email must be valid format
- Phone must be +91 followed by 10 digits
- Custom goal amount (if selected) must be between ₹1,000 and ₹10,00,000
- Personal message max 500 characters
- Show inline error messages

**Server-Side:**

- Re-validate all fields
- Check for duplicate fundraisers (same email within 24 hours)
- Sanitize inputs (prevent SQL injection, XSS)
- Rate limiting: Max 3 fundraiser creations per IP per day

**Security:**

- reCAPTCHA v3 (optional but recommended)
- Honeypot field (hidden, catch bots)
- CSRF protection
- HTTPS/SSL required

***

### **ON FORM SUBMISSION:**

**Step 1: Generate Unique Fundraiser**

- Create unique fundraiser ID (e.g., `FR-20260215-ABCD1234`)

### **ON FORM SUBMISSION:**

**Step 1: Create Fundraiser**

- Generate unique fundraiser ID: `FR-YYYYMMDD-XXXX` (e.g., FR-20260215-AB12)
- Generate unique shareable URL: `rkm.foundation/f/FR-20260215-AB12`
- Create fundraiser page with submitted details

**Step 2: Save to Database**

```
Fundraiser Table:
- fundraiser_id (unique)
- name
- email
- phone
- occasion
- goal_amount
- cause_type
- personal_message
- created_date
- status (active/closed)
- total_raised (starts at 0)
- donation_count (starts at 0)
```

**Step 3: Zoho CRM Integration**

```json
{
  "Lead_Source": "Website - Fundraiser Creation",
  "Lead_Status": "Fundraiser Created",
  "Lead_Owner": "[Assign to Karan]",
  "Full_Name": "[User Name]",
  "Email": "[Email]",
  "Phone": "[Phone]",
  "Custom_Field_Occasion": "[Occasion]",
  "Custom_Field_Goal": "[Goal Amount]",
  "Custom_Field_Cause": "[Cause Type]",
  "Tag": ["Fundraiser Creator"]
}
```

**Step 4: Send Confirmation Email**

**To:** [User Email]
**From:** info@rkm.support
**Subject:** Your fundraiser is live! Here's your link

**Email Body:**

```
Hi [Name],

Your fundraiser is live! 🎉

Here's your unique link to share:
[Fundraiser URL]

What's next?
1. Share your link on WhatsApp, Instagram, Facebook
2. Use the message templates below
3. Track donations on your dashboard: [Dashboard Link]

WhatsApp Message Template:
[Copy-paste template from page]

Instagram Caption Template:
[Copy-paste template from page]

Questions? WhatsApp us: +91 99207 80005

Let's create impact together!

Team RKM Foundation
www.rkm.foundation
```

**Step 5: Internal Notification**

**To:** info@rkm.support
**Subject:** New Fundraiser Created - [Name]

```
New fundraiser created:

Name: [Name]

Phone: [Phone]

Goal: ₹[Amount]
Cause: [Cause Type]
Message: [Personal Message]

```

### **SECURITY \& COMPLIANCE:**

**Data Protection:**

- All donor data encrypted
- PCI-DSS compliant (Razorpay handles payment)
- HTTPS/SSL for all pages
- Secure database storage

**Fundraiser Safety:**

- Only RKM-run causes allowed
- No image upload (prevents misuse)
- No custom HTML (prevents phishing)
- Moderation: Review flagged fundraisers

**Legal Compliance:**

- All funds to RKM Foundation directly
- No peer-to-peer transfers
- 80G receipts issued by RKM (not individuals)
- Compliant with Indian fundraising laws

## 🎯 **STARTING: DONATE PAGE**

***

# **DONATE PAGE - FORMAT \& STRUCTURE PROPOSAL**


***

## **DONOR PERSPECTIVE (Putting on "Donor Hat"):**

### **Who lands here?**

- Individual donors (25-45 years old primarily)
- Emotional decision-makers (saw animal story, wants to help NOW)
- Needs simplicity (don't make me think)
- Wants to feel good (impact validation)
- May be skeptical (is this legit?)


### **What they need to see:**

1. ✅ **Immediate clarity** - What am I donating to?
2. ✅ **Preset amounts** - Don't make me decide, suggest amounts
3. ✅ **Impact proof** - What does my ₹1,000 actually DO?
4. ✅ **Trust signals** - 80G, legal, secure payment
5. ✅ **Choice** - Monthly vs one-time, cause selection
6. ✅ **No friction** - Fast, mobile-friendly, minimal fields
7. ✅ **Goal visibility** - Are others donating? Is this urgent?

### **What they DON'T need:**

- ❌ Long explanations (save for About page)
- ❌ Too many options (decision paralysis)
- ❌ Guilt-tripping (authentic, not manipulative)
- ❌ Complex forms (name, email, phone, amount - that's it)

***

## 📋 **DONATE PAGE STRUCTURE (10 SECTIONS):**


***

### **SECTION 1: HERO**

**Purpose:** Emotional hook + immediate CTA

**Elements:**

- Headline (emotional, action-oriented)
- Subheadline (what you're supporting)
- Image (rescued animal or shelter scene)
- Quick CTA (scroll to form)

***

### **SECTION 2: CHOOSE YOUR IMPACT (Donation Amounts)**

**Purpose:** Make decision easy with preset tiers + impact equivalents

**Elements:**

- 5-6 preset amounts (₹1K, ₹2K, ₹5K, ₹10K, ₹25K, Custom)
- Each amount shows specific impact
- Visual cards/boxes, clickable
- "Most popular" badge on one tier

***

### **SECTION 3: DONATION TYPE (One-Time vs Monthly)**

**Purpose:** Encourage recurring donations without pressure

**Elements:**

- Toggle or radio buttons
- One-time (default)
- Monthly recurring (with benefits highlighted)
- Simple, visual

***

### **SECTION 4: CHOOSE WHERE YOUR DONATION GOES**

**Purpose:** Give donors control over cause

**Elements:**

- Animal Shelter (permanent program)
- Current Month's Cause (if applicable)
- Where Needed Most (flexibility)
- Radio buttons or dropdown

***

### **SECTION 5: PAYMENT FORM**

**Purpose:** Collect minimal info, process payment

**Elements:**

- Name*
- Email*
- Phone*
- PAN (optional, for 80G)
- Payment method (Razorpay: UPI, Cards, Net Banking)
- Privacy note
- Submit/Donate button

***

### **SECTION 6: TRUST SIGNALS (Above or Near Form)**

**Purpose:** Reduce hesitation, prove legitimacy

**Elements:**

- 80G registered badge
- Secure payment icon
- "Instant receipt" message
- Legal credentials visible

***

### **SECTION 7: FIRST YEAR GOAL TRACKER**

**Purpose:** Create urgency, social proof

**Elements:**

- ₹12L goal
- Progress bar (₹X raised so far)
- Breakdown (₹7.5L animals, ₹3L community, ₹1.5L admin)
- Donor count (optional)

***

### **SECTION 8: WHY DONATE TO RKM (Optional, Keep Brief)**

**Purpose:** Quick trust-building for skeptical donors

**Elements:**

- 3-4 bullets
- 85-90% to programs
- Transparent reporting
- Volunteer-driven team
- 80G benefit

***

### **SECTION 9: FREQUENTLY ASKED QUESTIONS**

**Purpose:** Remove objections, clarify process

**Elements:**

- 5-7 quick Q\&As
- Is my donation secure?
- How do I get 80G receipt?
- Can I cancel monthly donation?
- Where exactly does my money go?
- Accordion format to save space

***

### **SECTION 10: ALTERNATE WAYS TO GIVE**

**Purpose:** Offer other engagement options

**Elements:**

- Start a fundraiser (link to Fundraiser page)
- Shop with purpose (link to Shop page)
- Corporate partnership (link to CSR page)
- Volunteer (if applicable)

***

## 🎯 **KEY DESIGN PRINCIPLES FOR DONATE PAGE:**

1. **Mobile-first** - Most donations happen on phone
2. **One-column flow** - Clear, linear path to donate
3. **Minimal distractions** - No navigation clutter once form starts
4. **Fast loading** - Payment page should load in <2 seconds
5. **Progress indication** - Show what step donor is on
6. **Exit intent** - Popup if they try to leave ("Sure you want to leave?")

***

## 📊 **PROPOSED PAGE FLOW (Linear):**

```
HERO (emotional hook)
    ↓
CHOOSE AMOUNT (₹1K, ₹2K, ₹5K, ₹10K, ₹25K)
    ↓
ONE-TIME or MONTHLY toggle
    ↓
CHOOSE CAUSE (Animal / Current / General)
    ↓
FORM (Name, Email, Phone, PAN optional)
    ↓
PAYMENT (Razorpay)
    ↓
THANK YOU PAGE
```

**Side Elements (Not blocking flow):**

- Trust badges (visible throughout)
- Goal tracker (sticky or visible)
- FAQ (below form, expandable)

***

- ✅ Donor-friendly (simple, clear, fast)

## 🎯 **STUDYING YOUR CONTENT - DONOR LENS ANALYSIS**


***

## ✅ **WHAT WORKS WELL:**

1. ✅ **Clear cause choice** (Animal Shelter vs This Month's Focus)
2. ✅ **One-time vs Monthly** (simple toggle)
3. ✅ **Preset amounts** with "Most chosen" social proof
4. ✅ **Anonymous donation option** (privacy-conscious donors appreciate this)
5. ✅ **PAN explanation** (clear why it's needed)
6. ✅ **Declaration** (legal compliance, builds trust)
7. ✅ **Alternative giving methods** (cheque, large contributions)
8. ✅ **Other ways to support** (volunteer, skills, resources)
9. ✅ **No ₹12L goal displayed** (smart - internal target only)

***

## ⚠️ **DONOR CONCERNS (What Needs Fixing):**

### **1. TOO MANY FORM FIELDS = DONATION DROP-OFF**

**Current fields:** 13 fields (Name, DOB, Email, Phone, Address, Pincode, City, State, Country, PAN, Anonymous checkbox)

**Donor thought:** *"Why do they need my birthday and full address? This feels invasive. Maybe I'll donate later..." [Never returns]*

**Industry standard for online donations:** 4-6 fields max

- Name
- Email
- Phone
- Amount
- (PAN optional)

**Address/DOB only needed for:**

- Large donations (₹2L+)
- Tax audit trail
- But NOT for standard ₹1K-₹25K donations

**Fix:** Make address \& DOB optional or conditional (only show if donation >₹2L)

***

### **2. PRESET AMOUNTS DON'T MATCH IMPACT TIERS**

**Current:** ₹2,500 | ₹5,000 | ₹10,000

**Problem:** These amounts don't align with your impact equivalents:

- ₹2,000 = Feed 1 dog/month
- ₹3,000 = Neuter male
- ₹5,000 = Medical emergency
- ₹7,000 = Neuter female
- ₹10,000 = Build 1 kennel

**Donor thought:** *"What does my ₹2,500 actually do? It's not ₹2,000 (feeding) or ₹3,000 (neutering)..."*

**Fix:** Use impact-aligned amounts:

- ₹2,000 (Feed 1 animal/month)
- ₹5,000 (Medical emergency) *Most chosen*
- ₹10,000 (Build 1 kennel)
- ₹25,000 (Support 1 animal/year)

***

### **3. "THIS MONTH'S FOCUS" = VAGUE**

**Current:** "Your donation supports our current focus, shown below / side"

**Donor thought:** *"What IS the current focus? I can't see it. Is there even one? Should I just pick Animal Shelter?"*

**Fix:** Either:

- Show actual current cause with name (e.g., "Education: School supplies for 50 kids")
- OR remove it if no active cause (don't show empty option)
- OR default to "Where needed most" (more honest)

***

### **4. DATE OF BIRTH = RED FLAG**

**Current:** Date of birth field (no explanation why)

**Donor thought:** *"Why do they need my birthday? Are they selling my data? This is weird."*

**Reality:** DOB might be needed for large donation tax audits, but for ₹1K-₹25K, it's overkill.

**Fix:** Remove DOB entirely OR make it conditional for donations >₹50K

***

### **5. DECLARATION SOUNDS SCARY**

**Current:** "By proceeding, you confirm that you are an Indian citizen and that the donation is made from your own funds."

**Donor thought:** *"Wait, what if I'm NRI? Can I not donate? Why do they need to confirm 'my own funds'—do they think I'm laundering money?"*

**Fix:** Soften language:

- "By donating, you confirm this contribution is from your own funds (required for tax compliance)."
- Remove "Indian citizen" (NRIs can donate to 80G NGOs, just no tax benefit)

***

### **6. ADDRESS COLLECTION = FRICTION**

**Current:** Full address, pincode, city, state, country

**Donor thought:** *"I just want to give ₹2,000 to feed a dog. Why do you need my home address?"*

**Reality:** Address only needed for:

- Physical 80G certificate delivery (but most prefer email)
- Large donations (audit trail)

**Fix:**

- Make address optional ("Want 80G certificate by post?" checkbox → then show address)
- OR collect just City/State (dropdown, not typed)

***

### **7. PAN = CONFUSING FOR SMALL DONORS**

**Current:** PAN field with explanation

**Donor doing ₹2,000 donation thought:** *"I don't have my PAN card handy. I'll come back later..." [Never returns]*

**Reality:**

- PAN needed for 80G certificate
- But instant receipt can be sent without PAN
- Donor can submit PAN later in same FY

**Fix:**

- PAN optional at donation time
- Email message: "Submit PAN anytime before March 31 to get 80G certificate"
- Reduces friction NOW, collects later

***

## ⚖️ **LEGAL \& COMPLIANCE CHECK - INDIAN NGO DONATION REQUIREMENTS**

Let me analyze from both legal compliance AND donor conversion perspective...

***

## 📋 **FIELD-BY-FIELD LEGAL ANALYSIS:**

### **1. ADDRESS - LEGALLY REQUIRED?**

**Legal Reality:**

- ✅ **YES for 80G certificate issuance** (Income Tax rules require donor address on certificate)
- ✅ **YES for donations >₹2,000 in cash equivalent** (but online is not cash, so grey area)
- ✅ **YES for audit trail** (FCRA, IT Act compliance)
- ❌ **NOT required for donation receipt** (instant acknowledgment)

**Conclusion:** **KEEP ADDRESS** but make it simpler:

- Full address (single text field, not broken into multiple)
- Pincode (auto-fill city/state)
- Enough for 80G certificate

**RECOMMENDATION:**

```
Address* (for 80G certificate)
[Single text box: Type full address]

Pincode*
[Auto-fills City & State]

City: [Auto-filled]
State: [Auto-filled]
```

**Reduces from 5 fields to 2 fields** (Address + Pincode), rest auto-filled.

***

### **2. DATE OF BIRTH - LEGALLY REQUIRED?**

**Legal Reality:**

- ❌ **NOT required** by Income Tax for 80G
- ❌ **NOT required** by FCRA
- ⚠️ **Only needed** for KYC if donation >₹10 lakh (large donor reporting)

**Conclusion:** **REMOVE DOB** for standard donations (₹1K-₹25K range)

**RECOMMENDATION:** Remove entirely. If someone donates >₹10L, collect via follow-up email.

***

### **3. PAN - LEGALLY REQUIRED?**

**Legal Reality:**

- ✅ **REQUIRED for 80G certificate** if donation >₹2,000 (Income Tax Rule 18AA)
- ❌ **NOT required for donation receipt**
- ✅ **Mandatory for tax deduction claim** (donor's responsibility, but you need it for certificate)

**Your concern:** "Some people don't provide PAN, then back-and-forth happens"

**SOLUTION - TWO-TIER APPROACH:**

**Option A: Make PAN required** (lose some donors who don't have it handy)

- PAN mandatory field
- Clear message: "PAN required for 80G tax certificate"
- If they don't have it → they leave, donation lost

**Option B: Make PAN optional WITH INSTANT CHOICE** (recommended)

**At PAN field, show this:**

```
PAN Number (optional)

○ I have my PAN - I want 80G tax certificate
   [Enter PAN: _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _]

○ I don't have my PAN right now - Just give me a donation receipt
   (No 80G certificate, but you can submit PAN later via email before March 31)

Clear explanation below:
✓ With PAN: You get 80G certificate (50% tax deduction)
✓ Without PAN: You get instant donation receipt (no tax benefit unless you email PAN later)
```

**Why Option B is better:**

- ✅ Doesn't lose donor in the moment (they can still donate NOW)
- ✅ Clear choice (they know what they're getting)
- ✅ Door open for later (can email PAN within FY)
- ✅ No back-and-forth (they chose upfront)

**My strong recommendation: Option B**

***

### **4. NRI DONORS - HOW TO HANDLE?**

**Legal Reality:**

- ✅ NRIs CAN donate to 80G NGOs
- ❌ NRIs CANNOT get 80G tax benefit (Indian tax benefit only)
- ⚠️ If you don't have FCRA license, you CANNOT accept foreign currency
- ✅ But NRIs can donate from Indian bank accounts (₹ INR)

**Your situation:** No FCRA license = Can accept from NRIs ONLY if:

- Payment in INR (not USD/GBP/EUR)
- From Indian bank account OR Indian payment method
- No foreign currency transfer

**SOLUTION:**

**In Declaration section, rewrite:**

**BEFORE:**
> "By proceeding, you confirm that you are an Indian citizen and that the donation is made from your own funds."

**AFTER:**
> "By donating, you confirm:
> - This donation is from your own funds (required for tax compliance)
> - Payment is in Indian Rupees (INR) from an India-based payment method
> - (Note: 80G tax benefit available only for Indian taxpayers)"

**Why this works:**

- ✅ Allows NRIs donating in INR from Indian accounts (legal)
- ✅ Blocks foreign currency (FCRA compliance)
- ✅ Clarifies 80G is for Indian taxpayers only
- ✅ Not discriminatory, just factual

***

## ✅ **FINAL FIELD STRUCTURE - LEGALLY COMPLIANT + CONVERSION OPTIMIZED:**

### **REVISED FORM FIELDS (8 fields, down from 13):**

| Field | Type | Required | Legal Reason | Donor Impact |
| :-- | :-- | :-- | :-- | :-- |
| **Full Name** | Text | Yes | 80G certificate, receipt | Standard |
| **Email** | Email | Yes | Receipt delivery, communication | Standard |
| **Mobile** | Phone | Yes | Updates, verification | Standard |
| **Address** | Text area | Yes | 80G certificate requirement | Single field, not 5 |
| **Pincode** | Number | Yes | Auto-fill city/state, 80G cert | Auto-fill reduces typing |
| **City** | Auto-filled | - | 80G certificate | No donor action |
| **State** | Auto-filled | - | 80G certificate | No donor action |
| **PAN (Optional with choice)** | Text + Radio | Conditional | 80G certificate if provided | Clear choice upfront |
| **Anonymous** | Checkbox | No | Privacy preference | Donor control |

**Fields REMOVED:**

- ❌ Date of Birth (not needed for <₹10L donations)
- ❌ Country (implied by INR payment)
- ❌ Separate City/State typing (auto-filled from pincode)

**NET RESULT:**

- Donor types: Name, Email, Phone, Address, Pincode, PAN (if they want 80G)
- **6 fields actively typed** (down from 10)
- **Much better conversion** while staying 100% compliant

***

## 📋 **REVISED PAN SECTION:**

```
PAN Number (for 80G tax certificate)

Choose one option:

○ I have my PAN - Issue 80G certificate
   PAN: [_ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _]
   (You'll get 50% tax deduction)

○ I don't have my PAN - Issue donation receipt only
   (No 80G benefit now, but you can email PAN later before March 31 for certificate)

Why we ask: PAN is mandatory for 80G tax certificates (Income Tax Rule 18AA)
```


***

## 🎯 **MY FINAL RECOMMENDATIONS:**

### **1. Address:** KEEP (single field + pincode)

**Legally required for 80G certificate**

### **2. Date of Birth:** REMOVE

**Not legally required for standard donations**

### **3. PAN:** OPTIONAL WITH CLEAR CHOICE

**Two-tier: "I have PAN" (get 80G) OR "No PAN" (get receipt, submit later)**

### **4. NRI Handling:** DECLARATION REWRITE

**Allow INR donations, clarify 80G for Indian taxpayers only, block foreign currency**

### **5. Preset Amounts:** ₹2,000 | ₹5,000 (Most chosen) | ₹10,000 | ₹25,000

**Impact-aligned, clear value proposition**

### **6. Anonymous:** CHECKBOX, UNCHECKED BY DEFAULT

**Most donors want recognition, but option available**

### **7. "This Month's Focus":** AUTO-SYNC FROM HOME PAGE

**Always show (you confirmed there's always an active cause)**

***

## ✅ **DOES THIS APPROACH WORK?**

**It balances:**

- ✅ Legal compliance (80G, IT Act, audit trail)
- ✅ Donor conversion (fewer fields, clear choices)
- ✅ No back-and-forth (PAN choice made upfront)
- ✅ NRI-friendly (INR donations allowed, 80G clarified)
- ✅ Privacy (anonymous option, address only for 80G)

**Approve this structure and I'll write the complete Donate page content?**

### **SECTION 13: FREQUENTLY ASKED QUESTIONS (OPTIONAL - ACCORDION)**

**Section Headline:**
Frequently asked questions

**Q: Is my donation secure?**
A: Yes. We use Razorpay, a certified secure payment gateway. Your payment details are encrypted and never stored on our servers.

**Q: How do I get my 80G certificate?**
A: If you provide your PAN, your 80G certificate will be emailed within 48 hours. You can claim 50% tax deduction on your donation.

**Q: Can I cancel my monthly donation?**
A: Yes, anytime. Just email info@rkm.support and we'll process it immediately—no questions asked.

**Q: Where exactly does my money go?**
A: 85-90% goes directly to programs (animal care, community support). The remaining 10-15% covers essential administration and fundraising. Full transparency in our annual reports.

**Q: Can I donate if I'm an NRI?**
A: Yes, as long as you pay in Indian Rupees (INR) from an India-based payment method. Note: 80G tax benefit is only for Indian taxpayers.

**Q: What if I don't have my PAN right now?**
A: No problem. Choose "I don't have my PAN" and you'll get a donation receipt. You can email your PAN anytime before March 31 to receive your 80G certificate.

**Q: Will I get updates on how my donation was used?**
A: Yes! You'll receive periodic email updates with photos and stories showing the impact of your contribution.

**Legal Compliance:** ✅ 80G requirements met, NRI-friendly, FCRA compliant

## 🎯 **KEY IMPROVEMENTS FROM ORIGINAL:**

| **Element** | **Original** | **Revised** | **Why** |
| :-- | :-- | :-- | :-- |
| **Date of Birth** | Required | Removed | Not legally needed, reduces friction |
| **Address fields** | 5 separate fields | 2 fields (Address + Pincode, rest auto-fill) | Faster, less typing |
| **PAN** | Unclear/required | Optional with clear choice | No back-and-forth, donor decides upfront |
| **NRI language** | "Indian citizen only" | "INR payment, 80G for Indian taxpayers" | Legally accurate, inclusive |
| **Preset amounts** | ₹2,500, ₹5,000, ₹10,000 | ₹2,000, ₹5,000, ₹10,000, ₹25,000 | Impact-aligned, clear value |
| **Anonymous** | Not mentioned position | Checkbox, unchecked default | Privacy option, most want recognition |
| **Declaration** | Scary legal language | Simplified, factual | Less intimidating, clear |


***

## ✅ **READY FOR IMPLEMENTATION?**

**This version:**

- ✅ Legally compliant (80G, IT Act, FCRA)
- ✅ Donor-friendly (8 fields, clear choices, no friction)
- ✅ Conversion-optimized (preset amounts, trust signals, mobile-first)
- ✅ No back-and-forth (PAN choice made upfront)
- ✅ NRI-inclusive (INR donations allowed, 80G clarified)
- ✅ Impact-focused (every amount shows specific outcome)

## ⚖️ **LEGAL CLARITY ON INTERNATIONAL DONATIONS**

You're right - if you don't have FCRA license, you **CANNOT accept foreign currency donations at all** (not even from NRIs abroad).

Let me clarify the legal scenarios:

***

## 🌍 **DONATION SCENARIOS:**

### **✅ ALLOWED (Without FCRA):**

1. Indian citizen donating in INR from Indian bank
2. NRI donating in INR from their NRE/NRO account (Indian bank)
3. NRI in India temporarily, donating via Indian payment method

### **❌ NOT ALLOWED (Without FCRA):**

1. NRI sending money from US/UK/UAE bank account in foreign currency
2. Foreign citizen donating from abroad
3. Any donation originating outside India in foreign currency

***

## ✍️ **HOW TO WRITE THIS CLEARLY (3 OPTIONS):**


***

### **OPTION A: SIMPLE \& DIRECT** ⭐ *Recommended*

**For Donate Page:**

**Declaration section:**
> **By donating, you confirm:**
> - This donation is from your own funds
> - Payment is being made from an India-based bank account or payment method in Indian Rupees (INR)
> - We cannot accept donations from foreign bank accounts or in foreign currency
>
> *(80G tax benefit available only for Indian taxpayers)*

***

**For Fundraiser Page:**

**In "How It Works Safely" section, add:**
> **Important:** All donations must be made from India-based payment methods in Indian Rupees (INR). We cannot accept international transfers or foreign currency donations.

***

### **OPTION B: FRIENDLY \& EXPLANATORY**

**For Donate Page:**

**Declaration section:**
> **Before you donate:**
> - Donations must be made in Indian Rupees (INR)
> - Payment must be from an India-based bank account or payment method
> - We cannot process international transfers or foreign currency (we don't have FCRA approval)
>
> *(If you're an NRI, you can donate from your Indian bank account. 80G benefit applies only to Indian taxpayers.)*

***

**For Fundraiser Page:**

**In "How It Works Safely" section:**
> **Payment requirements:** To comply with Indian regulations, we can only accept donations made in Indian Rupees (INR) from India-based payment methods. International transfers are not permitted.

***

### **OPTION C: LEGAL \& COMPREHENSIVE** (More formal)

**For Donate Page:**

**Declaration section:**
> **Donation compliance requirements:**
>
> By proceeding, you confirm:
> - Payment is being made in Indian Rupees (INR) only
> - Payment originates from an India-based bank account or payment gateway
> - You understand that RKM Foundation does not hold FCRA (Foreign Contribution Regulation Act) approval and therefore cannot accept donations from foreign sources
>
> *(NRIs may donate from their Indian bank accounts (NRE/NRO). 80G tax benefit available to Indian taxpayers only.)*

***

**For Fundraiser Page:**

**Add new FAQ:**

**Q: Can international supporters donate?**
A: We currently accept donations only in Indian Rupees (INR) from India-based payment methods. As we don't have FCRA approval, we cannot process international bank transfers or foreign currency donations. NRIs can donate from their Indian bank accounts.

***

## 🎯 **MY RECOMMENDATION:**

**Use OPTION A** because:

- ✅ Clear and direct
- ✅ Not intimidating (no legal jargon like "FCRA")
- ✅ Explains what IS allowed (India-based payment in INR)
- ✅ Explains what ISN'T (foreign bank/currency)
- ✅ Short enough not to scare donors
- ✅ Legally accurate

***

## 📋 **FINAL WORDING - OPTION A:**

### **FOR DONATE PAGE (Declaration Section):**

```
Declaration & privacy

By donating, you confirm:
• This donation is from your own funds
• Payment is being made from an India-based bank account or payment method in Indian Rupees (INR)
• We cannot accept donations from foreign bank accounts or in foreign currency

(80G tax benefit available only for Indian taxpayers)

All information is kept strictly confidential and used only for regulatory compliance.
```


***

### **FOR FUNDRAISER PAGE (How It Works Safely Section):**

**Current text:**
> To keep fundraisers safe and compliant with Indian laws, all funds go directly to RKM Foundation's animal shelter programs that we run and monitor. You can't create fundraisers for other causes or upload unrelated content. This protects you, your donors, and the animals.
>
> Simple | Safe | Transparent.

**Add this:**
>
> **Payment requirements:** All donations must be made from India-based payment methods in Indian Rupees (INR). International transfers are not accepted.

**Final Section 8 text:**

```
How it works safely

To keep fundraisers safe and compliant with Indian laws, all funds go directly to RKM Foundation's animal shelter programs that we run and monitor. 

You can't create fundraisers for other causes or upload unrelated content. This protects you, your donors, and the animals.

All donations must be made from India-based payment methods in Indian Rupees (INR). International transfers are not accepted.

Simple | Safe | Transparent.
```


***

### **FOR FUNDRAISER PAGE (Optional - Add to FAQ):**

```
Q: Can my friends abroad donate to my fundraiser?
A: Donations must be made in Indian Rupees (INR) from India-based payment methods. Friends living abroad can donate if they have an Indian bank account, but we cannot accept international bank transfers or foreign currency.
```


***

## ✅ **DOES THIS WORDING WORK?**

**It accomplishes:**

- ✅ Blocks foreign currency (FCRA compliance)
- ✅ Allows NRIs with Indian accounts (legal and inclusive)
- ✅ Clear what's allowed vs not allowed
- ✅ Not scary or overly legal
- ✅ Consistent across Donate + Fundraiser pages

### **SECTION 12: FREQUENTLY ASKED QUESTIONS**

**Section Headline:**
Frequently asked questions

**Accordion Format (All Collapsed by Default):**

**Q: Is my donation secure?**
A: Yes. We use Razorpay, a certified secure payment gateway. Your payment details are encrypted and never stored on our servers.

**Q: How do I get my 80G certificate?**
A: If you provide your PAN, your 80G certificate will be emailed within 48 hours. You can claim 50% tax deduction on your donation.

**Q: Can I cancel my monthly donation?**
A: Yes, anytime. Just email info@rkm.support and we'll process it immediately—no questions asked.

**Q: Where exactly does my money go?**
A: 85-90% goes directly to programs (animal care, community support). The remaining 10-15% covers essential administration and fundraising. Full transparency in our annual reports.

**Q: Can I donate if I'm an NRI?**
A: Yes, as long as you pay in Indian Rupees (INR) from an India-based payment method. Note: 80G tax benefit is only for Indian taxpayers.

**Q: What if I don't have my PAN right now?**
A: No problem. Choose "I don't have my PAN" and you'll get a donation receipt. You can email your PAN anytime before March 31 to receive your 80G certificate.

**Q: Will I get updates on how my donation was used?**
A: Yes! You'll receive periodic email updates with photos and stories showing the impact of your contribution.

### **SECTION 12: FREQUENTLY ASKED QUESTIONS**

**Section Headline:**
Frequently asked questions

**7 Q\&As (Accordion Format - All Collapsed by Default):**

**Q: Is my donation secure?**
A: Yes. We use **Razorpay**, a **certified secure payment gateway**. Your payment details are **encrypted** and **never stored** on our servers.

**Q: How do I get my 80G certificate?**
A: If you provide your **PAN**, your **80G certificate** will be emailed **within 48 hours**. You can claim **50% tax deduction** on your donation.

**Q: Can I cancel my monthly donation?**
A: Yes, **anytime**. Just email info@rkm.support and we'll process it **immediately—no questions asked**.

**Q: Where exactly does my money go?**
A: **85-90% goes directly to programs** (animal care, community support). The remaining **10-15% covers essential administration and fundraising**. Full transparency in our annual reports.

**Q: Can I donate if I'm an NRI?**
A: Yes, as long as you pay in **Indian Rupees (INR)** from an **India-based payment method**. Note: **80G tax benefit is only for Indian taxpayers**.

**Q: What if I don't have my PAN right now?**
A: No problem. Choose **"I don't have my PAN"** and you'll get a **donation receipt**. You can email your PAN **anytime before March 31** to receive your **80G certificate**.

**Q: Will I get updates on how my donation was used?**
A: Yes! You'll receive **periodic email updates** with **photos and stories** showing the **impact of your contribution**.

**Design Notes:**

- Accordion format (click question to expand answer)
- All collapsed by default to save space
- +/- icons to show expand/collapse state
- Bold key terms in answers for scannability
- Mobile-friendly tap targets (min 44px)

- Amount buttons: 4 across in row
- Trust badges: Horizontal row
- Clean, spacious layout


### **Mobile (< 768px):**

- All form fields full-width, stacked
- Amount buttons: 2x2 grid

# **SHEET 2: TECH SPECIFICATIONS**


***

## **DONATE PAGE - TECHNICAL IMPLEMENTATION**

### **FORM CONFIGURATION:**

#### **Form Fields \& Validation:**

| Field Name | Type | Validation | Required | Max Length | Notes |
| :-- | :-- | :-- | :-- | :-- | :-- |
| Donation Cause | Radio | Pre-set: Animal Shelter / This Month's Focus | Yes | - | Default: Animal Shelter |
| Donation Type | Radio | One-time / Monthly | Yes | - | Default: One-time |
| Amount | Radio + Number | Pre-set OR custom (min ₹1,000) | Yes | 8 digits | Pre-set: 2500, 5000, 10000, 25000 |
| Anonymous | Checkbox | Boolean | No | - | Default: Unchecked |
| Full Name | Text | Letters, spaces, hyphens | Yes | 100 chars | - |
| Email | Email | Valid email format | Yes | 100 chars | - |
| Mobile | Phone | +91 + 10 digits | Yes | 13 chars | Auto-prefix +91 |
| Address | Textarea | Any text | Yes | 500 chars | For 80G certificate |
| Pincode | Number | 6 digits | Yes | 6 chars | Triggers auto-fill |
| City | Text | Auto-filled from pincode | Auto | 100 chars | Not editable by user |
| State | Text | Auto-filled from pincode | Auto | 100 chars | Not editable by user |
| PAN Option | Radio | Have PAN / Don't have PAN | Yes | - | Default: Have PAN |
| PAN Number | Text | 10 chars, format: AAAAA9999A | Conditional | 10 chars | Required if "Have PAN" selected |


***

### **FORM VALIDATION RULES:**

**Client-Side (Before Submit):**

- All required fields filled
- Email valid format
- Mobile: +91 + 10 digits
- Amount ≥ ₹1,000
- PAN format: 5 letters + 4 numbers + 1 letter (if provided)
- Pincode: exactly 6 digits
- Show inline error messages below each field

**Server-Side:**

- Re-validate all fields
- Check for SQL injection, XSS
- Sanitize all inputs
- Rate limit: Max 5 submissions per IP per hour

**Security:**

- reCAPTCHA v3 (recommended)
- Honeypot field (hidden)
- CSRF token
- HTTPS/SSL required

***

### **PINCODE AUTO-FILL FUNCTIONALITY:**

**On Pincode Input (6 digits entered):**

1. Trigger API call to pincode database (India Post API OR custom database)
2. Fetch City \& State

# Please note that if you do not provide your PAN Number, you will not be able to claim 50% tax exemption u/s 80G in India

this is what wry writes can we frame this in a more donor friendly way

Here are several donor-friendly ways to frame that PAN requirement message:

**OPTION 1 - BENEFIT FOCUSED (RECOMMENDED):**
"💰 Save on Taxes! Add your PAN to claim 50% tax deduction under Section 80G"

**OPTION 2 - HELPFUL TONE:**
"Want to claim your 50% tax benefit under 80G? Simply add your PAN number below"

**OPTION 3 - INFORMATIVE \& POSITIVE:**
"✓ Your PAN helps us issue your 80G certificate for 50% tax savings"

**OPTION 4 - CASUAL \& FRIENDLY:**
"Don't miss out! Share your PAN to get your 80G tax benefit (50% deduction)"

**OPTION 5 - CLEAR \& DIRECT:**
"Add PAN Number → Get 80G Certificate → Save 50% on Taxes"

**OPTION 6 - EMPOWERING:**
"Maximize your impact: Provide your PAN to receive 50% tax benefit under Section 80G"

**MY TOP RECOMMENDATION:**
"💡 **Add your PAN to unlock 50% tax savings under 80G**"

*Why this works:*

- **"Unlock"** = positive, benefit-oriented language (not "if you don't")
- **"Tax savings"** instead of "tax exemption" (savings sounds better to donors)
- Emoji makes it visually friendly
- No negative framing ("you will not be able to")
- Puts the BENEFIT first, not the requirement

Would you like me to refine any of these options further?

SECTION 12: FREQUENTLY ASKED QUESTIONS
Section Headline:
Frequently asked questions
7 Q\&As (Accordion Format - All Collapsed by Default):
Q: Is my donation secure?
A: Yes. We use Razorpay, a certified secure payment gateway. Your payment details are encrypted and never stored on our servers.
Q: How do I get my 80G certificate?
A: If you provide your PAN, your 80G certificate will be emailed within 48 hours. You can claim 50% tax deduction on your donation.
Q: Can I cancel my monthly donation?
A: Yes, anytime. Just email [info@rkm.support](mailto:info@rkm.support) and we'll process it immediately—no questions asked.
Q: Where exactly does my money go?
A: 85-90% goes directly to programs (animal care, community support). The remaining 10-15% covers essential administration and fundraising. Full transparency in our annual reports.
Q: Can I donate if I'm an NRI?
A: Yes, as long as you pay in Indian Rupees (INR) from an India-based payment method. Note: 80G tax benefit is only for Indian taxpayers.
Q: What if I don't have my PAN right now?
A: No problem. Choose "I don't have my PAN" and you'll get a donation receipt. You can email your PAN anytime before March 31 to receive your 80G certificate.
Q: Will I get updates on how my donation was used?
A: Yes! You'll receive periodic email updates with photos and stories showing the impact of your contribution.
Design Notes:
Accordion format (click question to expand answer)
All collapsed by default to save space
+/- icons to show expand/collapse state
Bold key terms in answers for scannability
Mobile-friendly tap targets (min 44px)

# **DONATE PAGE - REVISED IMPLEMENTATION SHEETS (ANALYZED \& REWRITTEN)**


***

## **SHEET 1: DESIGNER IMPLEMENTATION BRIEF**


***

### **PAGE OVERVIEW**

**Primary Goal:** Convert visitors into donors with ZERO unnecessary friction
**Design Philosophy:** Minimal distractions = Maximum conversions
**Style:** Clean, trustworthy, warm but not emotional manipulation
**Target Audience:** Individual donors (25-50 years), 65%+ mobile traffic
**Page Length:** Single scroll (~700 words max)
**Conversion Priority:** Animal Shelter (primary use case)

***

### **BRAND GUIDELINES**

**Typography:** Helvetica (all weights) - consistency with site
**Color Palette:**

- Primary: Black (\#000000)
- Secondary: Grey (\#666666, \#999999)
- Background: White (\#FFFFFF) or very light grey (\#F9F9F9)
- Accent: Warm color for CTAs (e.g., \#E67E22 orange or \#27AE60 green)

**Tone:** Trustworthy, transparent, impact-focused (not emotional guilt)
**Layout Principle:** Linear flow, generous whitespace, no sidebars/distractions

***

## **SECTION-BY-SECTION BREAKDOWN**


***

### **SECTION 1: HERO**

**Headline:**
Your generosity turns care into meaningful action

**Visual Element:**
Rescued animal image (dog or cat, warm, hopeful expression - NOT sad/pitiful)

**DONOR PSYCHOLOGY:**

- "Your" = personalized, donor is hero
- "Turns care into action" = concrete outcome, not vague help
- Warm image = emotional connection without guilt

**DESIGN SPECIFICATIONS:**

- Hero height: 60vh (desktop), 40vh (mobile)
- Image: Full-width, subtle gradient overlay for text contrast
- Headline: 48px (desktop), 32px (mobile), white text, centered
- No subheading (keep it clean)
- No CTA button in hero (reduces pressure, lets them read first)
- Mobile: Image above headline (stacked)

***

### **SECTION 2: CHOOSE WHERE YOUR DONATION GOES**

**Headline:**
Choose where your donation goes

**TWO OPTIONS (Large Radio Cards):**

**○ OPTION 1: Animal Shelter – Ongoing Care**

Your donation supports rescued animals with food, medical care, and shelter.

**Impact examples:**

- **₹2,000** – feeds one animal for a month
- **₹3,000** – neutering \& post-op care
- **₹5,000** – emergency medical treatment
- **₹10,000** – builds one kennel

***

**○ OPTION 2: This Month's Focus** [Badge: **Recommended**]

**[Auto-synced Current Cause Name from Home Page]**

Your donation supports our current priority cause.

***

**Note below (small, grey text):**
Both options are carefully planned and transparently tracked.

**TECHNICAL NOTE:**
"This Month's Focus" auto-syncs from Home page CMS. Single source of truth. Display method: One image + one line description for each option (Animal Shelter \& Monthly Focus). Developer to determine simplest implementation.

**DONOR PSYCHOLOGY:**

- **Choice = control = trust**
- "Recommended" nudges without forcing
- Specific impact amounts answer "what will my money actually do?"
- Short, punchy format (not paragraphs) for animal shelter
- "Carefully planned" = not random, not wasteful

**DESIGN SPECIFICATIONS:**

- **Radio cards:** Large (min 100px height), border style, NOT filled background
- **Selected state:** Thicker border (3px) + subtle accent color fill
- **Impact examples:** Indented 20px, grey text (\#666), smaller font (14px)
- **"Recommended" badge:** Small (80px width), warm accent color, positioned top-right of card
- **Spacing:** 30px between the two option cards
- **Touch target:** Entire card is clickable (not just radio button)
- **Mobile:** Cards stacked, full-width, 20px spacing

***

### **SECTION 3: CHOOSE HOW YOU'D LIKE TO GIVE**

**Headline:**
Choose how you'd like to give

**TWO OPTIONS (Radio Buttons - Simple Style):**

**○ One-time donation**

**○ Monthly donation** *(pause or cancel anytime by email)*

**DONOR PSYCHOLOGY:**

- Monthly positioned as **flexible**, not trap
- "Pause or cancel anytime" = commitment anxiety reducer
- "By email" = human, simple (not buried in settings)

**DESIGN SPECIFICATIONS:**

- Standard radio buttons (not large cards - keep it simple here)
- "pause or cancel anytime" in grey text, italic, not bold
- Optional icons: One-time (single heart), Monthly (two connected hearts)
- Spacing: 15px between options
- Mobile: Stacked

***

### **SECTION 4: CHOOSE AN AMOUNT**

**Headline:**
Choose an amount

**PRESET AMOUNTS (Clickable Cards):**

₹2,500  |  ₹5,000 [**Most chosen**]  |  ₹10,000  |  ₹25,000

**Custom Amount:**
Other amount: ₹ [__________]

**Note below (small, grey):**
Donations accepted from ₹1,000 onwards to maximize impact.

***

**☐ Make this donation anonymous**
*Your name will not be displayed publicly. Receipts and records will still be maintained.*

**DONOR PSYCHOLOGY:**

- **"Most chosen" = social proof** (₹5,000 sweet spot)
- Custom field = respects donor agency
- ₹1,000 minimum framed positively ("maximize impact" not "minimum requirement")
- Anonymous option = privacy respect
- "Receipts maintained" clarifies it's not shady

**DESIGN SPECIFICATIONS:**

- **Amount cards:** Equal size (120px width), border style, centered numbers
- **"Most chosen" badge:** Small banner above ₹5,000 card, accent color
- **Selected state:** Border + subtle fill color
- **Custom amount field:** Same visual weight as preset cards, ₹ symbol prefix
- **Anonymous checkbox:** Below custom amount, clear spacing, grey explanation text
- **Mobile:** 2x2 grid for presets, then custom field full-width below
- **Touch targets:** Min 48px height

***

### **SECTION 5: YOUR DETAILS**

**Headline:**
Your details

**FORM FIELDS:**


| **Field Label** | **Type** | **Required** | **Placeholder/Notes** |
| :-- | :-- | :-- | :-- |
| Full name | Text | Yes (*) | Enter your full name |
| Email | Email | Yes (*) | your.email@example.com |
| Mobile number | Phone | Yes (*) | 10-digit number (auto +91 prefix) |
| Address *(for 80G certificate)* | Textarea | Yes (*) | Enter your complete address |
| Pincode | Number | Yes (*) | 6 digits – City \& State will auto-fill |
| City | Text | Auto-filled | *(Auto-filled from pincode)* |
| State | Text | Auto-filled | *(Auto-filled from pincode)* |

**DONOR PSYCHOLOGY:**

- "Your details" sounds personal, not bureaucratic
- "(for 80G certificate)" explains WHY we need address
- Auto-fill = less work, faster completion
- Greyed-out auto-filled fields = clear they don't need to touch them

**DESIGN SPECIFICATIONS:**

- **Field spacing:** 20px vertical gap between fields
- **Required asterisk (*):** Red color, after label
- **Address textarea:** 4 rows minimum
- **Pincode field:** On blur (when user clicks away), trigger City/State auto-fill
- **City/State:** Greyed out (\#E0E0E0 background), not editable, italic placeholder text
- **Inline validation:**
    - Error: Red text below field + red border
    - Success: Green checkmark icon right side of field
- **Mobile:** Full-width fields, stacked, 16px font minimum (prevent iOS zoom)

***

### **SECTION 6: PAN FOR 80G CERTIFICATE**

**Headline:**
PAN for 80G certificate

**TWO OPTIONS (Radio Buttons):**

**○ I have my PAN**
PAN Number: [__________]
*(Format: AAAAA9999A)*

**Please note:** We can issue 80G certificates only when PAN is provided, as per Income Tax guidelines.

***

**○ I don't have my PAN right now**

You'll receive a donation receipt. Email us your PAN anytime before March 31 to receive your 80G certificate.

**DONOR PSYCHOLOGY:**

- Two clear paths = no confusion
- "I don't have my PAN **right now**" = temporary, not shameful
- Option to send later = doesn't lose donation due to missing PAN
- "as per Income Tax guidelines" = government rule, not arbitrary
- March 31 deadline = clear, actionable

**DESIGN SPECIFICATIONS:**

- **Radio options:** Stacked vertically, 30px spacing
- **PAN input field:** Only appears when "I have my PAN" is selected (conditional display)
- **Format hint:** Grey text below field, 12px font
- **"Please note" box:** Light grey background (\#F5F5F5), 15px padding, not intimidating
- **Second option explanation:** Grey text, 14px, below radio button
- **Mobile:** Same layout

- We **cannot accept** foreign bank transfers or foreign currency
- **80G tax benefit** available for **Indian taxpayers only**

**All information is kept strictly confidential and used only for compliance.**

**DONOR PSYCHOLOGY:**

- Bullet format = scannable
- Bold key terms = skim-friendly
- "Strictly confidential" + "only for compliance" = privacy + no spam
- Sets expectations (prevents NRI complaints later)

**DESIGN SPECIFICATIONS:**

- **Bullets:** Clean, 20px spacing between items
- **Bold terms:** Use <strong> tag, not just CSS
- **Font:** 14px, grey text (\#666)
- **Optional:** Light grey background box with 20px padding
- **NOT red/warning colors** – just informative grey
- **Mobile:** Same layout

### **SECTION 12: FREQUENTLY ASKED QUESTIONS**

**Headline:**
Frequently asked questions

**ACCORDION FORMAT (All Collapsed by Default):**

**Q1: Is my donation secure?**
Yes. We use Razorpay, a certified secure payment gateway. Your payment details are encrypted and never stored on our servers.

**Q2: How do I get my 80G certificate?**
If you provide your PAN, your 80G certificate will be emailed within **48 hours**. You can claim **50% tax deduction** on your donation.

**Q3: Can I cancel my monthly donation?**
Yes, anytime. Just email info@rkm.support and we'll process it immediately—**no questions asked**.

**Q4: Where exactly does my money go?**
**85-90% goes directly to programs** (animal care, community support). The remaining 10-15% covers essential administration and fundraising. Full transparency in our **annual reports**.

**Q5: Can I donate if I'm an NRI?**
Yes, as long as you pay in **Indian Rupees (INR)** from an **India-based payment method**. Note: 80G tax benefit is only for Indian taxpayers.

**Q6: What if I don't have my PAN right now?**
No problem. Choose **"I don't have my PAN"** and you'll get a donation receipt. Email your PAN anytime **before March 31** to receive your 80G certificate.

**Q7: Will I get updates on how my donation was used?**

***

# **DONATE PAGE - SHEET 1: DESIGNER IMPLEMENTATION BRIEF**


***

## **PAGE OVERVIEW**

**Primary Goal:** Convert visitors into donors with ZERO unnecessary friction
**Design Philosophy:** Minimal distractions = Maximum conversions (especially for animal shelter)
**Style:** Clean, trustworthy, warm but professional
**Target Audience:** Individual donors (25-50 years), mobile-heavy users
**Page Length:** Single scroll page (~700 words total)
**Traffic:** 65%+ mobile, design mobile-first
**Key Principle:** Linear flow, no sidebars, no pop-ups, no distractions

***

## **BRAND GUIDELINES**

**Typography:**

- Font family: Helvetica (all weights) - consistent with site
- Hierarchy: Clear H1, H2, body text distinction

**Color Palette:**

- **Primary:** Black (\#000000) for text
- **Secondary:** Grey (\#666666 for body, \#999999 for notes)
- **Background:** White (\#FFFFFF) or very light grey (\#F9F9F9)
- **Accent:** Warm color for CTAs (recommended: \#E67E22 orange OR \#27AE60 green)

**Tone of Voice:**

- Trustworthy, transparent, impact-focused
- NOT guilt-driven or emotionally manipulative
- Clear, direct, helpful

**Layout Principles:**

- Linear vertical flow (top to bottom)
- Generous whitespace (breathing room)
- No sidebars, no distractions
- Single-column mobile layout

***

## **SECTION-BY-SECTION DESIGN SPECIFICATIONS**


***

### **SECTION 1: HERO**

**Copy:**

**Headline:**
Your generosity turns care into meaningful action

**Visual Element:**
Emotional animal/shelter image (rescued dog or cat, warm and hopeful expression)

***

**DONOR PSYCHOLOGY:**

- "Your generosity" = personalizes, makes donor the hero
- "Turns care into action" = concrete outcome, not vague "help"
- Warm animal image = emotional connection WITHOUT guilt/sadness
- No CTA in hero = reduces pressure, allows them to explore first

**DESIGN SPECIFICATIONS:**

**Desktop (1200px+):**

- Hero section: Full-width, 60vh height
- Image: Full-width background, subtle dark gradient overlay (20% opacity) for text contrast
- Headline:
    - Font: Helvetica Bold, 48px
    - Color: White
    - Position: Center-aligned, vertically centered
    - Max-width: 800px
- No subheading (keep clean)
- No CTA button in hero

**Mobile (<768px):**

- Hero section: 40vh height
- Headline: 32px font size
- Image: Same full-width, stacked above headline
- Padding: 20px horizontal

***

### **SECTION 2: CHOOSE WHERE YOUR DONATION GOES**

**Copy:**

**Section Headline:**
Choose where your donation goes

**Two Options (Large Radio Button Cards):**

***

**○ OPTION 1: Animal Shelter – Ongoing Care**

Your donation supports rescued animals with food, medical care, and shelter.

**Impact examples:**

- **₹2,000** – feeds one animal for a month
- **₹3,000** – neutering \& post-op care
- **₹5,000** – emergency medical treatment
- **₹10,000** – builds one kennel

***

**○ OPTION 2: This Month's Focus** [Badge: **Recommended**]

**[Auto-synced Current Cause Name from Home Page]**

Your donation supports our current priority cause.

***

**Note below options (small text):**
Both options are carefully planned and transparently tracked.

***

**TECHNICAL NOTE FOR DEVELOPER:**
"This Month's Focus" must auto-sync from Home page current cause. Do NOT create separate CMS field. Single source of truth = Home page CMS. Display method: Show one image + single line description for each option (Animal Shelter \& Monthly Focus). Simplest implementation to be finalized with developer.

***

**DONOR PSYCHOLOGY:**

- **Choice = control = higher trust**
- "Recommended" badge nudges without forcing
- Animal shelter impact examples answer "what will my ₹X actually do?"
- Short, punchy format (NOT paragraphs) optimized for animal shelter use case
- "Carefully planned" reassures it's not random/wasteful spending
- Specific rupee amounts make impact tangible and believable

**DESIGN SPECIFICATIONS:**

**Radio Button Cards:**

- Style: Large bordered cards (NOT filled background)
- Size: Min 120px height, full-width
- Border: 2px solid \#DDDDDD (default), 3px solid accent color (selected)
- Background: White (default), very light accent color tint (selected, 5% opacity)
- Padding: 25px
- Touch target: Entire card is clickable (not just radio circle)
- Radio circle: Top-left corner, 24px diameter

**Impact Examples:**

- Indentation: 30px from left
- Font: Helvetica Regular, 14px
- Color: Grey (\#666666)
- Line spacing: 1.6
- Rupee amounts: Bold

**"Recommended" Badge:**

- Position: Top-right corner of Option 2 card
- Size: 90px width × 28px height
- Background: Accent color
- Text: White, uppercase, 11px
- Border radius: 4px

**Note Text:**

- Font: 12px, grey (\#999999), italic
- Position: Below both cards, centered
- Margin: 15px top

**Spacing:**

- Between two option cards: 25px
- Section padding: 60px top \& bottom (desktop), 40px (mobile)

**Mobile (<768px):**

- Cards: Stacked, full-width
- Same design, just vertical layout
- Badge: Smaller (80px width)

### **SECTION 5: YOUR DETAILS**

**Copy:**

**Section Headline:**
Your details

**Form Fields:**


| **Field Label** | **Type** | **Required** | **Placeholder/Note** |
| :-- | :-- | :-- | :-- |
| Full name | Text | Yes (*) | Enter your full name |
| Email | Email | Yes (*) | your.email@example.com |
| Mobile number | Phone | Yes (*) | 10-digit number |
| Address *(for 80G certificate)* | Textarea | Yes (*) | Enter your complete address |
| Pincode | Number | Yes (*) | 6 digits – City \& State will auto-fill |
| City | Text | Auto-filled | *(Auto-filled from pincode)* |
| State | Text | Auto-filled | *(Auto-filled from pincode)* |


***

**DONOR PSYCHOLOGY:**

- "Your details" sounds personal, not bureaucratic ("Enter information" would be cold)
- "(for 80G certificate)" explains WHY address is needed (transparency reduces suspicion)
- Pincode auto-fill = less work, faster completion, modern UX
- Greyed-out auto-filled fields = clear they don't need to touch them
- Mobile number prefix +91 auto-added = convenience

**DESIGN SPECIFICATIONS:**

**Form Layout:**

- Single column (mobile), 2-column where logical (desktop: Name/Email side-by-side, City/State side-by-side)
- Field spacing: 20px vertical gap between fields
- Max-width: 600px (desktop), centered or left-aligned

**Field Styling:**

- Height: 48px (text inputs), 120px (address textarea)
- Border: 1px solid \#DDDDDD (default), 2px solid accent color (focus)
- Background: White
- Font: 16px (prevents iOS auto-zoom)
- Padding: 15px inside
- Border radius: 4px

**Required Asterisk (*):**

- Color: Red (\#E74C3C)
- Position: After field label
- Font: 14px

**Address Textarea:**

- Rows: 4 minimum
- Resizable: Vertical only

**Pincode Field:**

- On blur (user clicks away after entering 6 digits): Trigger API call to auto-fill City \& State
- Loading state: Show small spinner in City/State fields while fetching

**City \& State Fields:**

- Background: Light grey (\#F5F5F5) when auto-filled
- Not editable (disabled state)
- Placeholder text: "(Auto-filled from pincode)" in grey italic
- If pincode invalid/not found: Show error message, allow manual entry

**Mobile Number:**

- Auto-prefix: "+91 " (not editable)
- User enters 10 digits only
- Format as they type: +91 XXXXX-XXXXX

**Inline Validation:**

- **Error state:**
    - Red text below field
    - Red border on field
    - Message: "Please enter a valid [field name]"
- **Success state:**
    - Small green checkmark icon (16px) on right side of field
    - Green border (optional, can be subtle)

**Spacing:**

- Section padding: 50px top \& bottom
- Between field label and input: 8px

**Mobile (<768px):**

- All fields: Full-width, stacked vertically
- Name/Email: Not side-by-side, stacked
- City/State: Not side-by-side, stacked

- **80G tax benefit** available for **Indian taxpayers only**

### **SECTION 12: FREQUENTLY ASKED QUESTIONS**

**Copy:**

**Section Headline:**
Frequently asked questions

**7 Q\&As (Accordion Format - All Collapsed by Default):**

***

**Q1: Is my donation secure?**
Yes. We use Razorpay, a certified secure payment gateway. Your payment details are encrypted and never stored on our servers.

**Q2: How do I get my 80G certificate?**
If you provide your PAN, your 80G certificate will be emailed within **48 hours**. You can claim **50% tax deduction** on your donation.

**Q3: Can I cancel my monthly donation?**
Yes, anytime. Just email info@rkm.support and we'll process it immediately—**no questions asked**.

**Q4: Where exactly does my money go?**
**85-90% goes directly to programs** (animal care, community support). The remaining 10-15% covers essential administration and fundraising. Full transparency in our **annual reports**.

**Q5: Can I donate if I'm an NRI?**
Yes, as long as you pay in **Indian Rupees (INR)** from an **India-based payment method**. Note: 80G tax benefit is only for Indian taxpayers.

**Q6: What if I don't have my PAN right now?**
No problem. Choose **"I don't have my PAN"** and you'll get a donation receipt. Email your PAN anytime **before March 31** to receive your 80G certificate.

**Q7: Will I get updates on how my donation was used?**
Yes! You'll receive **periodic email updates** with photos and stories showing the impact of your contribution.

***

**DONOR PSYCHOLOGY:**

- Accordion = clean, not overwhelming with all text visible
- Questions address TOP 7 donor objections/concerns:

1. Security (trust)
2. Tax benefit (financial incentive)
3. Cancellation (commitment anxiety)
4. Transparency (where money goes)
5. NRI eligibility (clarity)
6. PAN flexibility (reduces friction)
7. Impact proof (accountability)
- Bold key phrases = scannable even when expanded
- Answers are direct, honest, specific (no vague corporate-speak)

**DESIGN SPECIFICATIONS:**

**Accordion Layout:**

- All questions collapsed by default
- Click question to expand/collapse
- One question open at a time OR multiple can be open (multiple is better UX)

**Question Styling:**

- Font: 16px, bold, black
- Background: Light grey (\#F5F5F5) when collapsed, white when expanded
- Padding: 20px
- Border: 1px solid \#DDDDDD
- Cursor: Pointer
- Hover: Slightly darker background
- Icon: + icon (collapsed), - icon (expanded), positioned right side
- Border radius: 4px

**Answer Styling:**

- Font: 15px, grey (\#666666)
- Padding: 20px (left, right, bottom), 10px (top)
- Background: White
- Border: 1px solid \#DDDDDD (left, right, bottom only)
- Line height: 1.7

# HOW TO EXPORT THE WHOLE DATA TO THE NEW CHAT - ALSO IF I MOVE TO BUSINESS PRO - WILL I BE ABLE TO USE THIS CHAT PROPERLY ?

I'll answer both your questions:

***

## **1. HOW TO EXPORT THIS WHOLE CHAT DATA:**

**OPTION A: Copy-Paste Method (Immediate)**

1. Click the **three dots menu** (⋮) at the top of this chat
2. Select **"Export conversation"** or **"Copy conversation"**
3. This will copy the entire conversation to your clipboard
4. Open your new chat and paste it there
5. Note: This preserves text but may not preserve perfect formatting

**OPTION B: Share Link Method**

1. Click **"Share"** button in chat interface
2. Generate a share link
3. Open the link in a new tab/session
4. Reference it in your new chat by saying "Continue from this conversation: [link]"

**OPTION C: Manual Summary Method (Most Reliable)**
In your new chat, provide this context:

```
I'm continuing work on RKM Foundation NGO website. We've completed:

1. About Us page - approved final content
2. Donate page - currently working on implementation sheets

Current task: Complete DONATE PAGE implementation sheets:
- Sheet 1: Designer Implementation Brief (Section 12 in progress)
- Sheet 2: Tech Specifications (pending)

Key decisions made:
- Minimal distractions design philosophy
- Animal shelter as primary use case
- Mobile-first (65%+ traffic)
- PAN line: "Please note: We can issue 80G certificates only when PAN is provided, as per Income Tax guidelines."
- Two-path PAN system (have PAN / don't have PAN right now)
- Impact examples format: "₹2,000 - feeds one animal for a month"

Please continue creating Sheet 1 from Section 12 (FAQ design specs), then create Sheet 2 (Tech Implementation).
```


***

## **2. BUSINESS PRO COMPATIBILITY:**

**YES - Moving to Business Pro will work properly with this chat because:**

✅ **Chat history is preserved** - All conversations transfer across plan tiers
✅ **Browser automation tools remain available** - Business Pro includes all current tools
✅ **Longer context window** - Business Pro actually gives you MORE capacity
✅ **Better performance** - Faster responses, higher priority processing
✅ **More usage limits** - Higher message caps, more actions per session

**What Business Pro ADDS (doesn't break existing):**

- Team collaboration features
- Shared workspaces
- Priority support
- Advanced analytics
- Higher usage limits
- More concurrent tabs

**You won't lose:**

- This conversation history
- Your work-in-progress
- Any tool functionality
- Page content we've created

***

## **MY RECOMMENDATION:**

**For continuing THIS specific work:**

1. **Bookmark this chat** (so you can reference it)
2. **Export conversation** using Option A above
3. **In new chat, paste the summary** (Option C - cleaner)
4. **Reference**: "Continue Donate page Sheet 1 from Section 12"

**OR**

Just continue in **THIS CHAT** - I can finish the remaining sections:

- Section 12 FAQ design specs (just the tail end)
- Responsive design requirements
- Visual assets needed
- Then move to Sheet 2: Tech Implementation

***

**Which would you prefer?**

1. **Continue here** (I'll finish Sheet 1 now, then Sheet 2)
2. **Export and move to new chat**
3. **Wait until after you upgrade to Business Pro**

Let me know and I'll proceed accordingly!
